	GER_bismarck = {

		allowed = {
            tag = GER
        }

        cost = 0
        fire_only_once = yes

        available = {
            tag = GER
            has_tech = ger_battleship_3
            OR = {
				has_idea = MTG_anglo_german_naval_agreement
				has_completed_focus = GER_burn_the_naval_treaty
			}
        }

        visible = {
            original_tag = GER
			OR = {
				has_idea = MTG_anglo_german_naval_agreement
				has_completed_focus = GER_burn_the_naval_treaty
			}
			is_ai = no
        }

        complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ger_battleship_hull_3
						creator = "GER"
					}
					name = "Bismarck"
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.6
					amount = 1
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ger_battleship_hull_3
						creator = "GER"
					}
					name = "Tirpitz"
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.5
					amount = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ger_battleship_hull_3
						creator = "GER"
					}
					name = "Bismarck"
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0.1
					amount = 1
				}
				add_equipment_production = {
					equipment = {
						type = ger_battleship_hull_3
						creator = "GER"
					}
					name = "Tirpitz"
					requested_factories = 1
					progress = 0
					amount = 1
				}
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}

	GER_assume_control_of_resources = {

		icon = generic_industry

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}

		targets = { RAM RAT RBA RBE RBK RBL RBU RCA RCZ RDI REF REN RFI RFR RGR RHO RHU RIC RIR RIT RKA RMI RMO RNA RNO ROS RPE RPO RPT RPZ RRO RSE RSI RSO RSP RSW RTK RTU RUA RUK } #RDE

		target_root_trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_form_the_reichskommissariats
		}

		target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject_of = GER
				NOT = { has_country_flag = resources_taken_flag }
				OR = {
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = oil
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = iron
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = bauxite
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = rubber
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = coal
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = chromium
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = steel
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = aluminium
						amount > 0
					}
					has_resources_in_country = {
						resource = tungsten
						amount > 0
					}
				}
			}
		}

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 0

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 4000
		}

		complete_effect = {
			FROM = {
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_assume_control_of_resources_tt
				set_country_flag = resources_taken_flag
				hidden_effect = {
					every_controlled_state = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = oil
									amount > 0
								}
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = iron
									amount > 0
								}
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = bauxite
									amount > 0
								}
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = rubber
									amount > 0
								}
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = coal
									amount > 0
								}
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = chromium
									amount > 0
								}
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = steel
									amount > 0
								}
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = aluminium
									amount > 0
								}
								has_resources_amount = {
									resource = tungsten
									amount > 0
								}
							}
						}
						add_to_array = { FROM.state_array = THIS.id }
					}
					for_each_loop = {
						array = FROM.state_array
						value = s
						give_resource_rights = {
							receiver = ROOT
							state = s
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		highlight_states = {

		}

		}
		available = {

				is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER
			}
			5 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = GER
			}

political_actions = {

	GER_pay_for_spanish_food = {
		icon = generic_consumer_goods

		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}

		available = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" }
				}
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = SPR
					NOT = { has_idea = SPR_usa_food_imports }
					NOT = { has_idea = SPR_sov_food_imports }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "La Resistance"
				}
				SPA = {
					NOT = { has_idea = SPR_usa_food_imports }
					NOT = { has_idea = SPR_sov_food_imports }
				}
			}
		}

		visible = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" }
				}
				any_other_country = {
					original_tag = SPR
					has_government = fascism
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					has_idea = SPR_agricultural_mishandlement_2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "La Resistance"
				}
				AND = {
					SPA = {
						OR = {
							has_government = fascism
							has_government = neutrality
						}
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						has_idea = SPR_agricultural_mishandlement_2
					}
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 25

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 40
		}

		complete_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_pay_for_spanish_food_tt
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_dlc = "La Resistance" }
				}
				random_other_country = {
					limit = {
						original_tag = SPR
						OR = {
							has_government = fascism
							has_government = neutrality
						}
					}
					add_ideas = SPR_ger_food_imports
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "La Resistance"
				}
				SPA = {
					add_ideas = SPR_ger_food_imports
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_ruk_grain
				}
				remove_ideas = GER_ruk_grain
				add_ideas = GER_famine_payments_ukraine
			}
			else = {
				add_ideas = GER_famine_payments
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			
		}
	}

	GER_repay_loans_slowly = {
		icon = hol_attract_foreign_investors

		allowed = {
			original_tag = GER
		}

		available = {
		}

		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_recognizing_the_debt
			OR = {
				has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended
				has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_2
				has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_3
				has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_4
			}
		}

		days_remove = 120

		cost = 25

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 40
		}

		complete_effect = {
			add_ideas = GER_paying_off_debt_small
		}

		remove_effect = {
			remove_ideas = GER_paying_off_debt_small
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_4
				}
				remove_ideas = GER_mefo_bills_ended_4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_3
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_3
					add_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_2
					add_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended
					add_idea = GER_mefo_bills_ended_2
				}
			}
		}
	}

				}

							owner = {
								NOT = {
									tag = AUS
								}
								NOT = {
									is_in_faction_with = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_state_core = 853
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						997 = {
							owner = {
								NOT = {
									tag = AUS
								}
								NOT = {
									is_in_faction_with = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
					add_state_core = 997
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_country_flag = GER_anschluss_flag
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ger_civil_war_anschluss
				}
				unlock_national_focus = GER_stoke_the_fire_of_rebellion
				country_event = { id = ger_armor.210 }
			}
		}
	}

		icon = {

			trigger = {

				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = ger_garrison_control_1
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { GER_garrison_control = 0 }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = GER_fascist_stronghold }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = ger_garrison_control_2
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { GER_garrison_control = 1 }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = GER_fascist_stronghold }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = ger_garrison_control_3
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { GER_garrison_control = 2 }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = GER_fascist_stronghold }
				}
			}
		}
		icon = {
			key = opp_garrison_control_4
			trigger = {
				FROM = {
					check_variable = { var = GER_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					NOT = { has_state_flag = GER_fascist_stronghold }
				}
			}
		}

		allowed = {
			tag = GER
		}

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = GER_expand_influence_trigger_tt
				FROM = {
					check_variable = {
						GER_garrison_control < 3
					}
					any_neighbor_state = {
						check_variable = {
							GER_garrison_control > 2
						}
					}
					NOT = { has_state_flag = GER_fascist_stronghold }
				}
			}
		}

		state_target = yes

		on_map_mode = map_only

		target_array = GER.core_states
    	target_trigger = {
			FROM = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
			}
		}

		cost = 10

		days_remove = 28

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = GER_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = GER_civil_war_imminent_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					has_decision = GER_sway_armor_division_loyalty
					has_decision = GER_sway_infantry_division_loyalty
					has_decision = GER_sway_navy_loyalty
					has_decision = GER_sway_airforce_loyalty
					has_decision = GER_sway_army_leader_loyalty
					has_decision = GER_sway_navy_leader_loyalty
				}
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_expand_influence_tt
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = {
					add_to_variable = {
						GER_garrison_control = 1
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							check_variable = {
								GER_garrison_control = 2
							}
						}
						set_state_flag = FRA_opposition_state_flag
					}
				}
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GER_hitler_suspicion
				days = -7
			}
		}
	}
